 bain karavat par sone se hote hai ye phaayde-1

 ayurveda ke mutabik, bain karavat par sone se sehat acchhee bani rahati he, kyonki is pojishan main sone se sharir ke organ behatar tareeke se kaam karte hai
 2
 dil hamaari bain taraf hota he or jab aap usee taraf karavat lekar sote hai, to isse dil par pressure kam padhata he or dil sehatmand rahata he
 3
 bain taraf sone se digeshan bhi behatar hota he
 In fact, sleeping on the left side, sleeping, the material present in the body easily reaches from the small intestine to the large intestine
 iske baad west material sharir se aasaani se baahar nikal jaataa he or vyakti ko pet sambandhi samasyaayein hone kaa khatra kam hota he
 3
 health export ke mutabik, garbhvatee mahilaon ko zyada se zyada apni bain ore hi sona chahie
 In fact, during pregnancy, sleeping on the left side reduces the pressure on the waist of women and also the flow of blood in the uterus and fetus correctly
 bain taraf sone se sabhi nutrients placenta tak bhi aasaani se pahunch jate hai
 4
 aapako shaayad jaanakar hairaani hogi ki bain ore sone se kharraaton kii samasya kaaphi kam ho jaati he
 Actually, the tongue and throat remain in neutral position by sleeping on the left side, so that there is no problem in breathing while sleeping
 5
